He holds a Bachelor of Science and Masters of Science degrees in Industrial Engineering from the University of Central Florida, Orlando, Florida in 1978 and 1980 respectively. He also holds an MBA (Banking &amp; Finance) of the University of Lagos, Nigeria and an Advanced Management Diploma (AMP 15) of the prestigious Lagos Business School, Nigeria. He started his banking career in 1981 at the Nigerian Industrial Development Bank (now Bank of Industry) as an Industrial Engineer and was deployed to the Project Promotion &amp; Development Department. Mr. Ekere left the services of the Bank of Industry in 1987 and joined NAL Merchant Bank (now a member of the Sterling Bank Group) as an Assistant Manager in the Project Finance Unit. Here, he participated in the formulation and implementation of the World Bank assisted Infrastructure Development Fund and Health Systems Fund. He also participated, with the officials of The World Bank, in conducting prioritization studies, appraisals and supervision of projects for a number of participating state governments. At various times in NAL, he was placed in charge of a number of key Departments including, Treasury, Construction &amp; Public Sector, Financial Advisory Services and Investment Banking. He left the services of NAL in 2003 as a Deputy General Manager, and a well-rounded Investment Banker, to accept the appointment as Executive Director, Operations in NEXIM Bank. \u00a0At NEXIM Bank, Mr. Ekere managed the entire risk assets of the Bank and other business areas.
